002110GM_Object-sectionThere is an instance of table nested within example
<table id="GM_Object-section">
<name>GM_Object Class</name>
<tbody> <tr> <td valign="middle" align="left"> <p id="_9038f5ee-c98f-a977-162f-991c44267b96"> <strong>GM_Object</strong> </p>
</td>
</tr> <tr> <td valign="middle" align="left"> <table id="_38231cae-1665-5e7c-91f8-d2c9335852cb"> <colgroup> <col width="20%"/> <col width="80%"/> </colgroup> <tbody> <tr> <td valign="middle" align="left">    Definition:</td>


002114_38231cae-1665-5e7c-91f8-d2c9335852cbThere is an instance of table nested within example
<table id="_38231cae-1665-5e7c-91f8-d2c9335852cb"> <colgroup> <col width="20%"/> <col width="80%"/> </colgroup> <tbody> <tr> <td valign="middle" align="left">    Definition:</td>
<td valign="middle" align="left">GM_Object is the root class of the geometric object taxonomy and supports interfaces common to all geographically referenced geometric objects. GM_Object instances are sets of direct positions in a particular coordinate reference system. A GM_Object can be regarded as an infinite set of points that satisfies the set operation interfaces for a set of direct positions, TransfiniteSet&lt;DirectPosition&gt;. Since an infinite collection class cannot be implemented directly, a Boolean test for inclusion shall be provided by the GM_Object interface. This international standard concentrates on vector geometry classes, but future work may use GM_Object as a root class without modification.
NOTE As a type, GM_Object does not have a well-defined default state or value representation as a data type. Instantiated subclasses of GM_Object will.</td>
</tr> <tr> <td valign="middle" align="left">    Subclass Of:</td>
<td valign="middle" align="left">none</td>

<td valign="middle" align="left">GM_Object is the root class of the geometric object taxonomy and supports interfaces common to all geographically referenced geometric objects. GM_Object instances are sets of direct positions in a particular coordinate reference system. A GM_Object can be regarded as an infinite set of points that satisfies the set operation interfaces for a set of direct positions, TransfiniteSet&lt;DirectPosition&gt;. Since an infinite collection class cannot be implemented directly, a Boolean test for inclusion shall be provided by the GM_Object interface. This international standard concentrates on vector geometry classes, but future work may use GM_Object as a root class without modification.
NOTE As a type, GM_Object does not have a well-defined default state or value representation as a data type. Instantiated subclasses of GM_Object will.</td>

<tbody> <tr> <td valign="middle" align="left"> <p id="_dfde8217-6b19-7978-6820-fca67adf4536"> <strong>GenericName</strong> </p>
</td>
</tr> <tr> <td valign="middle" align="left"> <table id="_9c7126b1-f970-135f-b071-6102a670412a"> <colgroup> <col width="20%"/> <col width="80%"/> </colgroup> <tbody> <tr> <td valign="middle" align="left">    Definition:</td>


002672_9c7126b1-f970-135f-b071-6102a670412aThere is an instance of table nested within example
<table id="_9c7126b1-f970-135f-b071-6102a670412a"> <colgroup> <col width="20%"/> <col width="80%"/> </colgroup> <tbody> <tr> <td valign="middle" align="left">    Definition:</td>
<td valign="middle" align="left">Generic Name is the abstract class for all names in a NameSpace. Each instance of a GenericName is either a LocalName or a ScopedName. </tr> <tr> <td valign="middle" align="left">    StereoType:</td>

</td>
</tr> <tr> <td valign="middle" align="left"> <table id="_1932272a-edb7-4156-c2cd-946f54b58b7a"> <colgroup> <col width="20%"/> <col width="80%"/> </colgroup> <tbody> <tr> <td valign="middle" align="left">    Definition:</td>


002740_1932272a-edb7-4156-c2cd-946f54b58b7aThere is an instance of table nested within example
<table id="_1932272a-edb7-4156-c2cd-946f54b58b7a"> <colgroup> <col width="20%"/> <col width="80%"/> </colgroup> <tbody> <tr> <td valign="middle" align="left">    Definition:</td>
<td valign="middle" align="left">A Name Space is a domain in which “names” given by character strings (possibly under local constrains constraints enforced by the Name Space) can be mapped to objects via a getObejct operation. Examples include objects which form a Name Space for their attributes, operations and associations, or Schemas that form Name Spaces for their included data types or classes.
Not all methods for NameSpaces need to be made publicly accessible.</td>
</tr> <tr> <td valign="middle" align="left">    StereoType:</td>
<td valign="middle" align="left">interface</td>

000067conformance-sectionHanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="conformance-section" type="conformance" obligation="normative">
<title>Conformance</title>
<p id="_57fdae9d-6b9c-7964-fe9d-a6e86eaf2db9">This standard defines a <xref target="conceptual-model-definition">Conceptual Model</xref> which is independent of any encoding or formatting techniques.
The <xref target="standardization-target-definition">Standardization Target</xref> for this standard is technology-specific POI <xref target="implementation-specification-definition">Implementation Specifications</xref>.</p>

<clause id="poi_core-section" obligation="normative">
<title>POI Class Model</title>
<p id="_27d16bb9-3b88-ee83-65e3-70ee7ae90957">The following classes form the core of the POI model. These classes are the same for all POIs.</p>

000852data_​dictionary_​sectionHanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="data_dictionary_section" obligation="normative">
<title>POI Data Dictionary</title>
<p id="_9d533c05-cd55-ff96-9bbc-207a3d609b17">The POI UML model is the normative definition of the POI Conceptual Model. The Data Dictionary tables in this section were software generated from the UML model. As such, this section provides a normative representation of the POI Conceptual Model.</p>

002114_38231cae-1665-5e7c-91f8-d2c9335852cbTable should have title
<table id="_38231cae-1665-5e7c-91f8-d2c9335852cb"> <colgroup> <col width="20%"/> <col width="80%"/> </colgroup> <tbody> <tr> <td valign="middle" align="left">    Definition:</td>
<td valign="middle" align="left">GM_Object is the root class of the geometric object taxonomy and supports interfaces common to all geographically referenced geometric objects. GM_Object instances are sets of direct positions in a particular coordinate reference system. A GM_Object can be regarded as an infinite set of points that satisfies the set operation interfaces for a set of direct positions, TransfiniteSet&lt;DirectPosition&gt;. Since an infinite collection class cannot be implemented directly, a Boolean test for inclusion shall be provided by the GM_Object interface. This international standard concentrates on vector geometry classes, but future work may use GM_Object as a root class without modification.
NOTE As a type, GM_Object does not have a well-defined default state or value representation as a data type. Instantiated subclasses of GM_Object will.</td>
</tr> <tr> <td valign="middle" align="left">    Subclass Of:</td>
<td valign="middle" align="left">none</td>
